class="share-title">Share</h2> --> 		<a href="javascript:window.print();" class="share-print">Print</a> 	</div> </div> 		  	<div class="single-column"> 			    	<div class="box beige"> 		<h2 class="arrow-title brown large">new &amp; updated indicators</h2> 		<div class="indicators-list"> 											<ul> 					<li><p class="byline">Updated | June 26, 2015</p></li> 				</ul> 				<a href="http://kff.org/health-reform/state-indicator/total-monthly-medicaid-and-chip-enrollment/">Total Monthly Medicaid and CHIP&nbsp;Enrollment</a>											<ul> 					<li><p class="byline">Updated | June 26, 2015</p></li> 				</ul> 				<a href="http://kff.org/other/state-indicator/total-medicaid-and-chip-child-enrollment/">Monthly Child Enrollment in Medicaid and&nbsp;CHIP</a>											<ul> 					<li><p class="byline">Updated | June 02, 2015</p></li> 				</ul> 				<a href="http://kff.org/health-reform/state-indicator/premium-tax-credits-at-risk-in-king-v-burwell-supreme-court-decision/">Premium Tax Credits at Risk in King v. Burwell Supreme Court&nbsp;Decision</a>											<ul> 					<li><p class="byline">Updated | June 02, 2015</p></li> 				</ul> 				<a href="http://kff.org/health-reform/state-indicator/total-marketplace-enrollment-and-financial-assistance/">Total Marketplace Enrollment and Financial&nbsp;Assistance</a>											<ul> 					<li><p class="byline">Updated | June 02, 2015</p></li> 				</ul> 				<a href="http://kff.org/health-reform/state-indicator/marketplace-enrollment-as-a-share-of-the-potential-marketplace-population-2015/">Marketplace Enrollment as a Share of the Potential Marketplace&nbsp;Population</a>											<ul> 					<li><p class="byline">Updated | June 02, 2015</p></li> 				</ul> 				<a href="http://kff.org/health-reform/state-indicator/marketplace-enrollees-eligible-for-financial-assistance-as-a-share-of-subsidy-eligible-population/">Marketplace Enrollees Eligible for Financial Assistance as a Share of Subsidy-Eligible Population</a>						<!-- <a href="" class="see-more">View All Updates</a>	 --> 		</div>	 	</div> 			</div> 			<div class="right-column"> 							<div class="box beige"> 			    <h2 class="arrow-title dark-blue">data collection</h2> 				<h3> 					<a href="http://kff.org/data-collection/medicaid-benefits/"> 						Medicaid Benefits Data Collection					</a> 				</h3> 				<p>This data collection reflects Medicaid benefits covered in each state, limitations applied to those benefits, cost-sharing charges, and the reimbursement methodologies used for those benefits as of October 1, 2012.  Data for five additional points in time (January 1, 2003, October 1, 2004, October 1, 2006, October 1, 2008, and October 1, 2010) are also available.</p> 				<a href="http://kff.org/data-collection/medicaid-benefits/" class="see-more">View Data</a> 			</div> 					<div class="box beige"> 			    <h2 class="arrow-title dark-blue">data collection</h2> 				<h3> 					<a href="http://kff.org/data-collection/medicare-health-and-prescription-drug-plans/"> 						Medicare Health and Prescription Drug Plans					</a> 				</h3> 				<p>Data indicators about private plans participating in the Medicare Advantage program and the Medicare prescription drug program. The Medicare Health and Prescription Drug Plan Tracker enables users to monitor trends in enrollment, market penetration and other topics for Medicare Advantage plans since 1999 and stand-alone Medicare drug plans since 2006 by state, county and other sub-state geographies.</p> 				<a href="http://kff.org/data-collection/medicare-health-and-prescription-drug-plans/" class="see-more">View Data</a> 			</div> 					<div class="box beige"> 			    <h2 class="arrow-title dark-blue">data collection</h2> 				<h3> 					<a href="http://kff.org/data-collection/medicaid-managed-care-market-tracker/"> 						Medicaid Managed Care Market Tracker					</a> 				</h3> 				<p>More than half of Medicaid beneficiaries now receive all or most of their care from risk-based managed care organizations (MCO), and states are rapidly expanding their reliance on risk contracting. The Medicaid Managed Care Market Tracker houses extensive information about states, MCOs, and managed care firms to support understanding and analysis of the growing Medicaid managed care market.</p> 				<a href="http://kff.org/data-collection/medicaid-managed-care-market-tracker/" class="see-more">View Data</a> 			</div> 					</div> 		</div> 	</div> </div> </div>  <footer> 	 	<div
